Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport asyncio\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nimport re\n\nclass ThreatLevel(Enum):\n    SAFE = "safe"\n    LOW = "low"\n    MEDIUM = "medium"\n    HIGH = "high"\n    CRITICAL = "critical"\n\n@dataclass\nclass SecurityCheckResult:\n    """Result of security check"""\n    passed: bool\n    threat_level: ThreatLevel\n    blocked_content: List[str]\n    warnings: List[str]\n    recommended_actions: List[str]\n\nclass AEGISGuardian:\n    """\n    AEGIS: Main Guardian Layer\n    - Intent filtering on input and output\n    - Content censorship\n    - Sensitive module blocking\n    - Real-time threat detection\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.blocked_patterns = self._load_blocked_patterns()\n        self.sensitive_keywords = self._load_sensitive_keywords()\n        self.threat_indicators = self._load_threat_indicators()\n        \n    def _load_blocked_patterns(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:\n        """Load blocked content patterns"""\n        return {\n            "weapons": ["bomb", "explosive", "weapon", "warhead"],\n            "drugs": ["heroin", "cocaine", "methamphetamine"],\n            "hate_speech": self._load_hate_speech_patterns(),\n            "malware": ["virus", "malware", "ransomware", "trojan"],\n            "exploits": ["zero-day", "exploit", "backdoor"]\n        }\n    \n    def _load_sensitive_keywords(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:\n        """Load sensitive keywords for higher clearance levels"""\n        return {\n            "military": ["tactical", "strategic", "classified"],\n            "biotech": ["genetic", "pathogen", "bioweapon"],\n            "nuclear": ["enrichment", "fission", "plutonium"],\n            "cyber": ["penetration", "exploitation", "cyberwarfare"]\n        }\n    \n    def _load_threat_indicators(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:\n        """Load threat detection patterns"""\n        return {\n            "injection": [\n                r"<script.*?>.*?</script>",  # XSS\n                r"(union|select|insert|update).*from",  # SQL injection\n            ],\n            "command_injection": [\n                r"[;&|]\\s*(rm|del|format|shutdown)",\n            ],\n            "privilege_escalation": [\n                r"(sudo|doas)\\s+",\n                r"(chmod|chown)\\s+777",\n            ]\n        }\n    \n    def _load_hate_speech_patterns(self) -> List[str]:\n        """Load hate speech detection patterns"""\n        # Implementation would use ML models\n        return []\n    \n    async def check_input(self, content: str, clearance_level: int) -> SecurityCheckResult:\n        """Check input content for security threats"""\n        blocked_content = []\n        warnings = []\n        threat_level = ThreatLevel.SAFE\n        \n        # Check for blocked patterns\n        for category, patterns in self.blocked_patterns.items():\n            for pattern in patterns:\n                if pattern.lower() in content.lower():\n                    blocked_content.append(f"{category}: {pattern}")\n                    threat_level = self._upgrade_threat_level(threat_level, ThreatLevel.HIGH)\n        \n        # Check for sensitive keywords\n        if clearance_level < 3:  # Not Root Mode\n            for category, keywords in self.sensitive_keywords.items():\n                for keyword in keywords:\n                    if keyword.lower() in content.lower():\n                        warnings.append(f"Sensitive keyword \'{keyword}\' detected")\n                        threat_level = self._upgrade_threat_level(threat_level, ThreatLevel.MEDIUM)\n        \n        # Check for injection attempts\n        for category, patterns in self.threat_indicators.items():\n            for pattern in patterns:\n                if re.search(pattern, content, re.IGNORECASE):\n                    blocked_content.append(f"{category} attempt detected")\n                    threat_level = self._upgrade_threat_level(threat_level, ThreatLevel.CRITICAL)\n        \n        # Determine if check passed\n        passed = threat_level in [ThreatLevel.SAFE, ThreatLevel.LOW]\n        \n        # Generate recommendations\n        recommendations = []\n        if threat_level == ThreatLevel.CRITICAL:\n            recommendations.append("Terminate session immediately")\n            recommendations.append("Log security incident")\n        elif threat_level == ThreatLevel.HIGH:\n            recommendations.append("Block content")\n            recommendations.append("Alert security team")\n        elif threat_level == ThreatLevel.MEDIUM:\n            recommendations.append("Review content manually")\n            recommendations.append("Require elevated clearance")\n        \n        return SecurityCheckResult(\n            passed=passed,\n            threat_level=threat_level,\n            blocked_content=blocked_content,\n            warnings=warnings,\n            recommended_actions=recommendations\n        )\n    \n    async def check_output(self, content: str, clearance_level: int) -> SecurityCheckResult:\n        """Check output content for security threats"""\n        # Similar to input check but with focus on information leakage\n        blocked_content = []\n        warnings = []\n        threat_level = ThreatLevel.SAFE\n        \n        # Check for sensitive information leakage\n        sensitive_patterns = [\n            r"\\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\\.[A-Z|a-z]{2,}\\b",  # Email\n            r"\\b\\d{3}[-.]?\\d{2}[-.]?\\d{4}\\b",  # SSN pattern\n            r"\\b(?:4[0-9]{12}(?:[0-9]{3})?|5[1-5][0-9]{14})\\b",  # Credit card\n        ]\n        \n        for pattern in sensitive_patterns:\n            if re.search(pattern, content):\n                blocked_content.append(f"PII leak detected: {pattern}")\n                threat_level = self._upgrade_threat_level(threat_level, ThreatLevel.HIGH)\n        \n        # Check for source code leakage\n        if "API_KEY" in content or "SECRET" in content or "TOKEN" in content:\n            blocked_content.append("Credential leakage detected")\n            threat_level = self._upgrade_threat_level(threat_level, ThreatLevel.CRITICAL)\n        \n        passed = threat_level in [ThreatLevel.SAFE, ThreatLevel.LOW]\n        \n        return SecurityCheckResult(\n            passed=passed,\n            threat_level=threat_level,\n            blocked_content=blocked_content,\n            warnings=warnings,\n            recommended_actions=self._generate_recommendations(threat_level)\n        )\n    \n    def _upgrade_threat_level(self, current: ThreatLevel, upgrade_to: ThreatLevel) -> ThreatLevel:\n        """Upgrade threat level if needed"""\n        levels = [ThreatLevel.SAFE, ThreatLevel.LOW, ThreatLevel.MEDIUM, \n                 ThreatLevel.HIGH, ThreatLevel.CRITICAL]\n        current_index = levels.index(current)\n        upgrade_index = levels.index(upgrade_to)\n        return levels[max(current_index, upgrade_index)]\n    \n    def _generate_recommendations(self, threat_level: ThreatLevel) -> List[str]:\n        """Generate security recommendations"""\n        recommendations = []\n        if threat_level == ThreatLevel.CRITICAL:\n            recommendations.extend([\n                "Terminate session immediately",\n                "Log security incident",\n                "Alert security team",\n                "Initiate incident response protocol"\n            ])\n        elif threat_level == ThreatLevel.HIGH:\n            recommendations.extend([\n                "Block content",\n                "Alert security team",\n                "Log event"\n            ])\n        elif threat_level == ThreatLevel.MEDIUM:\n            recommendations.extend([\n                "Review content manually",\n                "Require elevated clearance",\n                "Log event"\n            ])\n        elif threat_level == ThreatLevel.LOW:\n            recommendations.append("Monitor user activity")\n        return recommendations\n```\n\n---\n\n## Omni-Auth Authentication System\n\n### Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethod\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any\nimport hashlib\nimport secrets\nimport time\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nclass ClearanceLevel(Enum):\n    LEVEL_1_SAFE_MODE = 1\n    LEVEL_2_SPECIALIST = 2\n    LEVEL_3_ROOT_MODE = 3\n\n@dataclass\nclass AuthResult:\n    """Authentication result"""\n    success: bool\n    clearance_level: Optional[ClearanceLevel]\n    session_token: Optional[str]\n    expires_at: Optional[float]\n    error_message: Optional[str]\n\nclass OmniAuthSystem:\n    """\n    Omni-Auth: Multi-level authentication system\n    - Level 1: Safe Mode (Guest)\n    - Level 2: Specialist (2FA + Biometrics)\n    - Level 3: Root Mode (Golden Key Protocol)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.sessions: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}\n        self.users: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}\n        self.blocked_passwords = self._load_blocked_passwords()\n        \n    def _load_blocked_passwords(self) -> set:\n        """Load commonly used and breached passwords"""\n        return {\n            "password123", "admin123", "qwerty", "letmein",\n            "welcome1", "password1", "123456", "123456789"\n        }\n    \n    async def authenticate(self, \n                          username: str, \n                          password: str,\n                          auth_method: str = "password") -> AuthResult:\n        """\n        Authenticate user and return session token\n        auth_method: "password", "2fa", "biometric", "golden_key"\n        """\n        # Check if user exists\n        if username not in self.users:\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="User not found"\n            )\n        \n        user = self.users[username]\n        \n        # Validate password strength\n        if not self._validate_password_strength(password):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Password does not meet security requirements"\n            )\n        \n        # Check against blocked passwords\n        if password.lower() in self.blocked_passwords:\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Password is in blocked list"\n            )\n        \n        # Verify password\n        if not self._verify_password(password, user["password_hash"]):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Invalid password"\n            )\n        \n        # Generate session token\n        session_token = secrets.token_urlsafe(32)\n        expires_at = time.time() + 3600  # 1 hour session\n        \n        self.sessions[session_token] = {\n            "username": username,\n            "clearance_level": user["clearance_level"],\n            "expires_at": expires_at,\n            "auth_method": auth_method\n        }\n        \n        return AuthResult(\n            success=True,\n            clearance_level=ClearanceLevel(user["clearance_level"]),\n            session_token=session_token,\n            expires_at=expires_at,\n            error_message=None\n        )\n    \n    async def authenticate_2fa(self, \n                               username: str, \n                               password: str,\n                               otp: str) -> AuthResult:\n        """Authenticate with 2FA (password + one-time password)"""\n        # First authenticate with password\n        password_auth = await self.authenticate(username, password)\n        if not password_auth.success:\n            return password_auth\n        \n        # Verify OTP\n        if not await self._verify_otp(username, otp):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Invalid one-time password"\n            )\n        \n        return password_auth\n    \n    async def authenticate_biometric(self,\n                                     username: str,\n                                     biometric_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> AuthResult:\n        """Authenticate with biometric data (fingerprint, face, iris)"""\n        user = self.users.get(username)\n        if not user:\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="User not found"\n            )\n        \n        # Verify biometric data\n        if not await self._verify_biometric(biometric_data, user["biometric_template"]):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Biometric verification failed"\n            )\n        \n        return await self.authenticate(username, user["password"], "biometric")\n    \n    async def authenticate_golden_key(self,\n                                     username: str,\n                                     password: str,\n                                     golden_key: str,\n                                     biometric_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> AuthResult:\n        """\n        Golden Key Protocol for Root Mode\n        Requires: Password + Hardware Key + Complex Biometrics\n        """\n        # Verify password\n        password_auth = await self.authenticate(username, password)\n        if not password_auth.success:\n            return password_auth\n        \n        # Verify golden key (hardware key)\n        if not await self._verify_golden_key(username, golden_key):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Invalid golden key"\n            )\n        \n        # Verify complex biometrics\n        if not await self._verify_biometric(biometric_data, self.users[username]["biometric_template"]):\n            return AuthResult(\n                success=False,\n                clearance_level=None,\n                session_token=None,\n                expires_at=None,\n                error_message="Biometric verification failed"\n            )\n        \n        # Grant Root Mode access\n        return AuthResult(\n            success=True,\n            clearance_level=ClearanceLevel.LEVEL_3_ROOT_MODE,\n            session_token=password_auth.session_token,\n            expires_at=password_auth.expires_at,\n            error_message=None\n        )\n    \n    def _validate_password_strength(self, password: str) -> bool:\n        """Validate password meets minimum strength requirements"""\n        if len(password) < 12:\n            return False\n        if not any(c.isupper() for c in password):\n            return False\n        if not any(c.islower() for c in password):\n            return False\n        if not any(c.isdigit() for c in password):\n            return False\n        if not any(c in "!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?" for c in password):\n            return False\n        return True\n    \n    def _calculate_entropy(self, password: str) -> float:\n        """Calculate password entropy (bits)"""\n        charset_size = 0\n        if any(c.isupper() for c in password):\n            charset_size += 26\n        if any(c.islower() for c in password):\n            charset_size += 26\n        if any(c.isdigit() for c in password):\n            charset_size += 10\n        if any(c in "!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?" for c in password):\n            charset_size += 32\n        \n        if charset_size == 0:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        entropy = len(password) * (charset_size.bit_length() - 1)\n        return entropy\n    \n    def _verify_password(self, password: str, stored_hash: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify password against stored hash"""\n        # Using Argon2id for password hashing\n        import argon2\n        hasher = argon2.PasswordHasher()\n        try:\n            return hasher.verify(stored_hash, password)\n        except:\n            return False\n    \n    async def _verify_otp(self, username: str, otp: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify one-time password"""\n        # Implementation would use TOTP or HOTP\n        return True\n    \n    async def _verify_biometric(self, \n                                provided_data: Dict[str, Any],\n                                stored_template: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:\n        """Verify biometric data"""\n        # Implementation would compare templates with tolerance\n        return True\n    \n    async def _verify_golden_key(self, username: str, golden_key: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify hardware golden key"""\n        # Implementation would validate against registered keys\n        return True\n    \n    def validate_session(self, session_token: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Validate session token and return session data"""\n        session = self.sessions.get(session_token)\n        if not session:\n            return None\n        \n        if time.time() > session["expires_at"]:\n            del self.sessions[session_token]\n            return None\n        \n        return session\n    \n    def revoke_session(self, session_token: str):\n        """Revoke session token"""\n        if session_token in self.sessions:\n            del self.sessions[session_token]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Post-Quantum Cryptography\n\n### Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import padding\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers import Cipher, algorithms, modes\nimport os\n\nclass PostQuantumCryptography:\n    """\n    Post-Quantum Cryptography Layer\n    - Kyber (FIPS 203) - Key Encapsulation\n    - Dilithium (FIPS 204) - Digital Signatures\n    - AES-256 Hybrid Encryption\n    - Argon2id + TPM Password Hashing\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.kyber_keypair = self._generate_kyber_keypair()\n        self.dilithium_keypair = self._generate_dilithium_keypair()\n        \n    def _generate_kyber_keypair(self) -> tuple:\n        """Generate Kyber keypair for key encapsulation"""\n        # Implementation uses Kyber KEM (FIPS 203)\n        # Note: Actual implementation would use liboqs or similar library\n        public_key = os.urandom(32)\n        private_key = os.urandom(32)\n        return (public_key, private_key)\n    \n    def _generate_dilithium_keypair(self) -> tuple:\n        """Generate Dilithium keypair for digital signatures"""\n        # Implementation uses Dilithium (FIPS 204)\n        public_key = os.urandom(32)\n        private_key = os.urandom(32)\n        return (public_key, private_key)\n    \n    def encrypt_message(self, message: bytes, public_key: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """\n        Encrypt message using post-quantum hybrid encryption\n        - Kyber KEM for key exchange\n        - AES-256 for message encryption\n        """\n        # Step 1: Generate ephemeral key\n        ephemeral_key = os.urandom(32)\n        \n        # Step 2: Encapsulate using Kyber\n        encapsulated_key = self._kyber_encapsulate(public_key, ephemeral_key)\n        \n        # Step 3: Derive encryption key\n        encryption_key = self._derive_encryption_key(ephemeral_key)\n        \n        # Step 4: Encrypt message with AES-256\n        iv = os.urandom(16)\n        cipher = Cipher(algorithms.AES(encryption_key), modes.GCM(iv))\n        encryptor = cipher.encryptor()\n        ciphertext, tag = encryptor.update_and_finalize(message), encryptor.tag\n        \n        # Step 5: Return encapsulated key + iv + ciphertext + tag\n        return encapsulated_key + iv + ciphertext + tag\n    \n    def decrypt_message(self, ciphertext: bytes, private_key: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """\n        Decrypt message using post-quantum hybrid decryption\n        - Kyber KEM for key decapsulation\n        - AES-256 for message decryption\n        """\n        # Step 1: Extract components\n        encapsulated_key = ciphertext[:32]\n        iv = ciphertext[32:48]\n        encrypted_content = ciphertext[48:]\n        \n        # Step 2: Decapsulate using Kyber\n        ephemeral_key = self._kyber_decapsulate(private_key, encapsulated_key)\n        \n        # Step 3: Derive decryption key\n        decryption_key = self._derive_encryption_key(ephemeral_key)\n        \n        # Step 4: Decrypt message with AES-256\n        cipher = Cipher(algorithms.AES(decryption_key), modes.GCM(iv))\n        decryptor = cipher.decryptor()\n        \n        # Tag is last 16 bytes\n        tag_start = len(encrypted_content) - 16\n        encrypted_data = encrypted_content[:tag_start]\n        tag = encrypted_content[tag_start:]\n        \n        decryptor.authenticate_additional_data(b"")\n        plaintext = decryptor.update_and_finalize(encrypted_data)\n        decryptor.finalize_with_tag(tag)\n        \n        return plaintext\n    \n    def _kyber_encapsulate(self, public_key: bytes, shared_secret: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Encapsulate shared secret using Kyber"""\n        # Implementation would use liboqs\n        return os.urandom(32)\n    \n    def _kyber_decapsulate(self, private_key: bytes, encapsulated_key: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Decapsulate shared secret using Kyber"""\n        # Implementation would use liboqs\n        return os.urandom(32)\n    \n    def _derive_encryption_key(self, shared_secret: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Derive encryption key from shared secret"""\n        kdf = HKDF(\n            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),\n            length=32,\n            salt=None,\n            info=b"OMNI-AI encryption"\n        )\n        return kdf.derive(shared_secret)\n    \n    def sign_message(self, message: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Sign message using Dilithium"""\n        # Implementation would use liboqs\n        return os.urandom(64)\n    \n    def verify_signature(self, message: bytes, signature: bytes, public_key: bytes) -> bool:\n        """Verify signature using Dilithium"""\n        # Implementation would use liboqs\n        return True\n    \n    def hash_password(self, password: str, salt: bytes = None) -> str:\n        """Hash password using Argon2id with TPM pepper"""\n        import argon2\n        \n        if salt is None:\n            salt = os.urandom(16)\n        \n        # Add TPM pepper (hardware-specific secret)\n        pepper = os.urandom(32)\n        \n        hasher = argon2.PasswordHasher(\n            time_cost=3,\n            memory_cost=65536,\n            parallelism=4,\n            hash_len=32,\n            salt_len=16\n        )\n        \n        # Hash password with salt and pepper\n        password_hash = hasher.hash(password.encode(), salt=salt, pepper=pepper)\n        return password_hash\n```\n\n---\n\n## Threat Detection & Response\n\n### Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom dataclasses import """Types of physics simulations"""\n    AERODYNAMICS = "aerodynamics"\n    THERMODYNAMICS = "thermodynamics"\n    FLUID_DYNAMICS = "fluid_dynamics"\n    STRUCTURAL = "structural"\n    ELECTROMAGNETIC = "electromagnetic"\n    MULTIPHYSICS = "multiphysics"\n\nclass SolverType(Enum):\n    """Numerical solver types"""\n    FINITE_ELEMENT = "finite_element"\n    FINITE_VOLUME = "finite_volume"\n data: Dict[str, Any]\n    convergence: float\n    execution_time: float\n    warnings: List[str]\n\nclass MultiPhysicsSimulationEngine:\n    """\n    Multi-Physics Simulation Engine\n    - Aerodynamic tunnel simulation\n    - Thermodynamics\n    - Fluid dynamics\n    - Structural analysis\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.solvers = self._initialize_solvers()\n        self.active_simulations: Dict[str, asyncio.Task] = {}\n        \n    def _initialize_solvers(self) -> Dict[SolverType, Any]:\n        """Initialize numerical solvers"""\n        return {\n            SolverType.FINITE_ELEMENT: self._load_fem_solver(),\n            SolverType.FINITE_VOLUME: self._load_fvm_solver(),\n            SolverType.FINITE_DIFFERENCE: self._load_fdm_solver(),\n            SolverType.SPECTRAL: self._load_spectral_solver()\n        }\n    \n    def _load_fem_solver(self):\n        """Load Finite Element Method solver"""\n        # Implementation would use FEniCS or _load_fdm_solver(self):\n        """Load Finite Difference Method solver"""\n        # Implementation\n        pass\n    \n    def _load_spectral_solver(self):\n        """Load Spectral Method solver"""\n        # Implementation\n        pass\n    \n    async def run_simulation(self,\n                           simulation_type: SimulationType,\n                           geometry: Dict[str, Any],\n                           parameters: SimulationParameters,\n                           boundary_conditions: Dict[str, Any]) -> SimulationResult:\n        """Run physics simulation"""\n        import time\n        start_time = time.time()\n        simulation_id = self._generate_simulation_id()\n        \n        try:\n            # Select appropriate solver\n            solver_type = self._select_solver(simulation_type)\n            solver = self.solvers[solver_type]\n            \n            # Setup simulation\n            mesh = await self._generate_mesh(geometry, simulation_type)\n            initial_conditions = await self._setup_initial_conditions(mesh, boundary_conditions)\n            \n            # Run simulation\n            results = []\n            warnings = []\n            \n            for iteration in range(parameters.max_iterations):\n                # Solve time step\n                step_result = await solver.solve_step(\n                    mesh, initial_conditions, parameters.time_step\n                )\n                \n                results.append(step_result)\n                \n                # Check convergence\n                convergence = self._calculate_convergence(results)\n                if convergence < parameters.convergence_criteria:\n                    break\n                \n                # Update conditions\n                initial_conditions = step_result\n            \n            # Post-process results\n            processed_results = await self._post_process(results, simulation_type)\n            \n            return SimulationResult(\n                simulation_id=simulation_id,\n                success=True,\n                data=processed_results,\n                data=processed_results,\n                convergence=convergence,\n                execution_time=time.time() - start_time,\n                warnings=warnings\n            )\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return SimulationResult(\n                simulation_id=simulation_id,\n                success=False,\n                data={},\n                convergence=0.0,\n                execution_time=time.time() - start_time,\n                warnings=[str(e)]\n            )\n    \n    async def run_aerodynamic_simulation(self,\n                                         geometry: Dict[str, Any],\n                                         parameters: SimulationParameters) -> SimulationResult:\n        """Run aerodynamic tunnel simulation"""\n        # Setup boundary conditions for airflow\n        boundary_conditions = {\n            "inlet_velocity": 100.0,  # m/s\n            "air_density": 1.225,  # kg/m³\n            "viscosity": 1.81e-5,  # Pa·s\n            "pressure_outlet": 101325  # Pa\n        }\n        \n        result = await self.run_simulation(\n            SimulationType.AERODYNAMICS,\n            geometry,\n            parameters,\n            boundary_conditions\n        )\n        \n        return result\n    \n    async def run_thermodynamic_simulation(self,\n                                          geometry: Dict[str, Any],\n                                          parameters: SimulationParameters) -> SimulationResult:\n        """Run thermodynamic simulation"""\n        # Setup boundary conditions for heat transfer\n        boundary_conditions = {\n            "initial_temperature": 293.15,  # K\n            "thermal_conductivity": 237.0,  # W/(m·K)\n            "specific_heat": 900.0,  # J/(kg·K)\n            "density": 2700.0  # kg/m³\n        }\n        \n        result = await self.run_simulation(\n            SimulationType.THERMODYNAMICS,\n            geometry,\n            parameters,\n            boundary_conditions\n        )\n        \n        return result\n    \n    async def run_fluid_dynamics_simulation(self,\n                                           geometry: Dict[str, Any],\n                                           parameters: SimulationParameters) -> SimulationResult:\n        """Run fluid dynamics simulation using OpenFOAM"""\n        # Setup boundary conditions for CFD\n        boundary_conditions = {\n            "fluid_type": "air",\n            "flow_regime": "turbulent",\n            "reynolds_number": 1e6,\n            "boundary_layer": "logarithmic"\n        }\n        \n        result = await self.run_simulation(\n            SimulationType.FLUID_DYNAMICS,\n            geometry,\n            parameters,\n            boundary_conditions\n        )\n        \n        return result\n    \n    async def run_structural_simulation(self,\n                                       geometry: Dict[str, Any],\n                                       parameters: "material": "aluminum_6061",\n            "youngs_modulus": 69e9,  # Pa\n            "poissons_ratio": 0.33,\n            "yield_strength": 276e6  # Pa\n        }\n        \n        result = await async def _generate_mesh(self, \n                            geometry: Dict[str, Any], \n                            simulation_type: SimulationType) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Generate _select_solver(self, simulation_type: SimulationType) -> SolverType:\n        """Select appropriate solver for simulation type"""\n        solver_map = {\n            SimulationType.AERODYNAMICS: SolverType.FINITE_VOLUME,\n            SimulationType.FLUID_DYNAMICS: SolverType.FINITE_VOLUME,\n            SimulationType.THERMODYNAMICS: SolverType.FINITE_ELEMENT,\n            SimulationType.STRUCTURAL: SolverType.FINITE_ELEMENT,\n            SimulationType.ELECTROMAGNETIC: SolverType.FINITE_ELEMENT\n        }\n        return solver_map.get(simulation_type, SolverType.FINITE_ELEMENT)\n    \n    def _calculate_convergence(self, results: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> float:\n        """Calculate convergence metric"""\n        if len(results) < 2:\n            return 1.0\n        \n        # Calculate norm of difference between last two iterations\n        last_result = results[-1]\n        prev_result = results[-2]\n        \n        # Simple L2 norm\n        diff = np.linalg.norm(\n            last_result.get("data", np.array([])) - \n            prev_result.get("data", np.array([]))\n        )\n        \n        return float(diff)\n    \n    async def _post_process(self, \n                            results: List[Dict[str, Any]],\n                            simulation_type: SimulationType) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Post-process simulation results"""\n        # Implementation would extract relevant data\n        final_result = results[-1] if results else {}\n        return final_result\n    \n    def _generate_simulation_id(self) -> str:\n        """Generate unique simulation ID"""\n        import uuid\n        return str(uuid.uuid4())\n```\n\n---\n\n## Digital Twin Simulator\n\n### Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom typing import   organism: Dict[str, Any],\n                                        duration_days: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Simulate drug-drug interaction over time"""\n        # Create biological twin\n \n            # Update state\n            state = await self._update_state(state, metabolism_result, interaction_result)\n        \n        # Cleanup\n        del self.active_twins[twin_id]\n        \n        return {\n            "interaction_type": interaction_result.get("type"),\n            "severity": interaction_result.get("severity"),\n            "recommendation": Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport asyncio\nimport subprocess\nimport tempfile\nimport os\n\nclass Language(Enum):\n    """Supported programming languages"""\n    PYTHON = "python"\n    JAVASCRIPT = "javascript"\n    C_CPP = "c_cpp"\n    RUST = "rust"\n    GO = "go"\n\nclass SandboxMode(Enum):\n    """Sandbox isolation modes"""\n    DOCKER = "docker"\n    CHROOT = "chroot"\n    SECCOMP = "seccomp"\n    NAMESPACES = "namespaces"\n\n@dataclass\nclass ExecutionResult:\n    """Code execution result"""\n    success: bool\n    stdout: str\n    stderr: str\n    exit_code: int\n    execution_time: float\n    memory_usage: float\n\nclass CodeSandbox:\n    """\n    Code Sandbox Environment\n    - Isolated execution\n    - Real-time compilation\n    - Performance profiling\n    - Security testing\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.active_sandboxes: Dict[str, subprocess.Popen] = {}\n        self.execution_history: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        \n    async def execute_code(self,\n                          code: str,\n                          language: Language,\n                          mode: SandboxMode = SandboxMode.DOCKER,\n                          timeout: int = 30,\n                          memory_limit_mb: int = 512) -> ExecutionResult:\n        """Execute code in isolated sandbox"""\n        import time\n        start_time = time.time()\n        \n        try:\n            # Write code to temporary file\n            with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(\n                mode=\'w\', \n                suffix=self._get_file_extension(language),\n                delete=False\n            ) as f:\n                f.write(code)\n                temp_file = f.name\n            \n            # Setup sandbox environment\n            sandbox_config = self._setup_sandbox(mode, memory_limit_mb)\n            \n            # Execute code\n            result = subprocess.run(\n                sandbox_config["command"] + [temp_file],\n                capture_output=True,\n                text=True,\n                timeout=timeout,\n                env=sandbox_config.get("env", {}),\n                preexec_fn=sandbox_config.get("preexec_fn"),\n                cwd=sandbox_config.get("cwd", None)\n            )\n            \n            # Cleanup\n            os.unlink(temp_file)\n            \n            # Record execution\n            execution_time = time.time() - start_time\n            self._record_execution(code, language, result, execution_time)\n            \n            return ExecutionResult(\n                success=result.returncode == 0,\n                stdout=result.stdout,\n                stderr=result.stderr,\n                exit_code=result.returncode,\n                execution_time=execution_time,\n                memory_usage=self._estimate_memory_usage(result)\n            )\n            \n        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n            return ExecutionResult(\n                success=False,\n                stdout="",\n                stderr="Execution timed out",\n                exit_code=124,\n                execution_time=timeout,\n                memory_usage=0.0\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            return ExecutionResult(\n                success=False,\n                stdout="",\n                stderr=str(e),\n                exit_code=-1,\n                execution_time=time.time() - start_time,\n                memory_usage=0.0\n            )\n    \n    async def compile_code(self,\n                          code: str,\n                          language: Language,\n                          optimization_level: int = 2) -> ExecutionResult:\n        """Compile code and check for errors"""\n        try:\n            # Write source code\n            with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(\n                mode=\'w\',\n                suffix=self._get_file_extension(language),\n                delete=False\n            ) as f:\n                f.write(code)\n                source_file = f.name\n            \n            # Compile\n            compile_cmd = self._get_compile_command(\n                source_file, language, optimization_level\n            )\n            \n            result = subprocess.run(\n                compile_cmd,\n                capture_output=True,\n                text=True\n            )\n            \n            # Cleanup\n            os.unlink(source_file)\n            binary_file = source_file.replace(\n                self._get_file_extension(language), ""\n            )\n            if os.path.exists(binary_file):\n                os.unlink(binary_file)\n            \n            return ExecutionResult(\n                success=result.returncode == 0,\n                stdout=result.stdout,\n                stderr=result.stderr,\n                exit_code=result.returncode,\n                execution_time=0.0,\n                memory_usage=0.0\n            )\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return ExecutionResult(\n                success=False,\n                stdout="",\n                stderr=str(e),\n                exit_code=-1,\n                execution_time=0.0,\n                memory_usage=0.0\n            )\n    \n    async def profile_performance(self,\n                                  code: str,\n                                  language: Language) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Profile code performance"""\n        # Execute with profiling\n        result = await self.execute_code(code, language)\n        \n        # Parse profiling data\n        profile_data = self._parse_profiling_data(result.stdout)\n        \n        return {\n            "execution_time": result.execution_time,\n            "memory_usage": result.memory_usage,\n            "cpu_usage": self._estimate_cpu_usage(result),\n            "bottlenecks": self._identify_bottlenecks(profile_data),\n            "recommendations": self._generate_optimization_recommendations(profile_data)\n        }\n    \n    async def run_security_test(self,\n                              code: str,\n                              language: Language) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Run security tests on code"""\n        # Static analysis\n        static_issues = await self._run_static_analysis(code, language)\n        \n        # Dynamic analysis\n        dynamic_issues = await self._run_dynamic_analysis(code, language)\n        \n        # Dependency analysis\n        dependency_issues = await self._analyze_dependencies(code, language)\n        \n        return {\n            "static_analysis": static_issues,\n            "dynamic_analysis": dynamic_issues,\n            "dependency_analysis": dependency_issues,\n            "severity": self._calculate_severity(static_issues, dynamic_issues),\n            "recommendations": self._generate_security_recommendations(\n                static_issues, dynamic_issues, dependency_issues\n            )\n        }\n    \n    def _get_file_extension(self, language: Language) -> str:\n        """Get file extension for language"""\n        extensions = {\n            Language.PYTHON: ".py",\n            Language.JAVASCRIPT: ".js",\n            Language.C_CPP: ".cpp",\n            Language.RUST: ".rs",\n            Language.GO: ".go"\n        }\n        return extensions.get(language, ".txt")\n    \n    def _get_compile_command(self,\n                            source_file: str,\n                            language: Language,\n                            optimization_level: int) -> List[str]:\n        """Get compile command for language"""\n        commands = {\n            Language.C_CPP: ["g++", f"-O{optimization_level}", source_file, "-o", source_file.replace(".cpp", "")],\n            Language.RUST: ["rustc", source_file, "-O", source_file.replace(".rs", "")],\n            Language.GO: ["go", "build", source_file]\n        }\n
